The KYDEX® 1-Piece Inside-the-Waistband (IWB) Standard Concealment Holster Making Kit with adjustable retention is a great way to go when you know what you want and only need enough material and parts to complete the design. This holster making kit contains everything you need to make a top quality IWB taco-style holster for the majority of handgun sizes. This holster making kit also comes with a Modwing to allow a user’s belt to apply additional leverage by rotating the holster and the grip of the gun towards the user’s body
creating better concealment and less user “printing” of the firearm and holster.  Also included are both printed and digital video instructions to help you successfully complete the project. You can follow step-by-step on how to create this 1-Piece IWB Concealment design (Sample Images Below). Whether you are a beginner who is just getting started or a professional who doesn't want the waste of unnecessary parts and materials
this holster making kit will provide you with a fantastic way to save time and money in your holster making process.
